# This file contains a list of debug tags followed by a source and a description.
# Each debug tag in the list is represented by the following elements:

#     #MSG=DEBUG TAG
#     COMMENT=description of debug tag
#     #:##SRC=SOURCE FILE : LINE NUMBER
#     #:##DEF=SOURCE CODE where DEBUG TAG was found

# For example:

#     68MSG=:Node:checkConditions
#     COMMENT=Notification of checking condition change or (possible) transition for a node.
#     68:1SRC=/home/laurel/plexil/universal-exec/Exec/base/Node.cc : 1243
#     68:1DEF=debugMsg("Node:checkConditions","Checking condition change for node " << m_nodeId.toString());
#     68:2SRC=/home/laurel/plexil/universal-exec/Exec/base/Node.cc : 1246
#     68:2DEF=debugMsg("Node:checkConditions","Can (possibly) transition to " << toState.toString());

# ':Node:checkConditions' is the 68th debug tag in the list and was found in
# two separate locations, thus the need for 68:1 and 68:2 SRC and DEF.
